\"istio.io/api/networking/v1alpha3\"\n    23→\t\"istio.io/istio/pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/provider\"\n    24→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config\"\n    25→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config/constants\"\n    26→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config/host\"\n    27→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config/labels\"\n    28→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config/protocol\"\n    29→\t\"istio.io/istio/pkg/config/schema/gvk\"\n    30→)\n    31→\n    32→const (\n    33→\twildcardNamespace = \"*\"\n    34→\tcurrentNamespace  = \".\"\n    35→\twildcardService   = host.Name(\"*\")\n    36→)\n    37→\n    38→var (\n    39→\tsidecarScopeKnownConfigTypes = map[config.GroupVersionKind]struct{}{\n    40→\t\tgvk.ServiceEntry:    {},\n    41→\t\tgvk.VirtualService:  {},\n    42→\t\tgvk.DestinationRule: {},\n    43→\t\tgvk.Sidecar:         {},\n    44→\t}\n    45→\n    46→\t// clusterScopedConfigTypes includes configs when they are in root namespace,\n    47→\t// they will be applied to all namespaces within the cluster.\n    48→\tclusterScopedConfigTypes = map[config.GroupVersionKind]struct{}{\n    49→\t\tgvk.EnvoyFilter:           {},\n    50→\t\tgvk.AuthorizationPolicy:   {},\n    51→\t\tgvk.RequestAuthentication: {},\n    52→\t}\n    53→)\n    54→\n    55→// SidecarScope is a wrapper over the Sidecar resource with some\n    56→// preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\n    57→// and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n    58→// sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n    59→// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n    60→// list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n    61→// SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n    62→// services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n    63→// wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n    64→// settings.\n    65→//\n    66→// Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n    67→// SidecarScope object. If the proxy's namespace does not have a user\n    68→// specified Sidecar CRD, we will construct one that has a catch all egress\n    69→// listener that imports every public service/virtualService in the mesh.\n    70→type SidecarScope struct {\n    71→\tName string\n    72→\t// This is the namespace where the sidecar takes effect,\n    73→\t// maybe different from the ns where sidecar resides if sidecar is in root ns.\n    74→\tNamespace string\n    75→\t// The crd itself. Can be nil if we are constructing the default\n    76→\t// sidecar scope\n    77→\tSidecar *networking.Sidecar\n    78→\n    79→\t// Version this sidecar was computed for\n    80→\tVersion string\n    81→\n    82→\t// Set of egress listeners, and their associated services.  A sidecar\n    83→\t// scope should have either ingress/egress listeners or both.  For\n    84→\t// every proxy workload that maps to a sidecar API object (or the\n    85→\t// default object), we will go through every egress listener in the\n    86→\t// object and process the Envoy listener or RDS based on the imported\n    87→\t// services/virtual services in that listener.\n    88→\tEgressListeners []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper\n    89→\n    90→\t// Union of services imported across all egress listeners for use by CDS code.\n    91→\tservices           []*Service\n    92→\tservicesByHostname map[host.Name]*Service\n    93→\n    94→\t// Destination rules imported across all egress listeners. This\n    95→\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\n    96→\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\n    97→\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\n    98→\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\n    99→\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\n   100→\t// destination rule.\n   101→\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n   102→\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\n   103→\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\n   104→\t// be forwarded.\n   105→\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n   106→\n   107→\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\n   108→\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\n   109→\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\n   110→\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\n   111→\n   112→\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\n   113→\t// Istio configuration.\n   114→\t//\n   115→\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\n   116→\tRootNamespace string\n   117→}\n   118→\n   119→// MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\n   120→func (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\n   121→\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\n   122→\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\n   123→\t\t\"version\":               sc.Version,\n   124→\t\t\"rootNamespace\":         sc.RootNamespace,\n   125→\t\t\"name\":                  sc.Name,\n   126→\t\t\"namespace\":             sc.Namespace,\n   127→\t\t\"outboundTrafficPolicy\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\n   128→\t\t\"services\":              sc.services,\n   129→\t\t\"sidecar\":               sc.Sidecar,\n   130→\t\t\"destinationRules\":      sc.destinationRules,\n   131→\t}, \"\", \"  \")\n   132→}\n   133→\n   134→// IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\n   135→// networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\n   136→// optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\n   137→// services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\n   138→type IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\n   139→\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\n   140→\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\n   141→\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\n   142→\n   143→\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\n   144→\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\n   145→\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\n   146→\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\n   147→\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\n   148→\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\n   149→\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\n   150→\tservices []*Service\n   151→\n   152→\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\n   153→\t// As with per listener services, this\n   154→\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\n   155→\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\n   156→\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. We need a\n   157→\t// virtualService set per listener and not one per sidecarScope because\n   158→\t// each listener imports an independent set of virtual services.\n   159→\t// Listener 1 could import a public virtual service for serviceA from\n   160→\t// namespace A that has some path rewrite, while listener2 could import\n   161→\t// a private virtual service for serviceA from the local namespace,\n   162→\t// with a different path rewrite or no path rewrites.\n   163→\tvirtualServices []config.Config\n   164→\n   165→\tlistenerHosts map[string][]host.Name\n   166→}\n   167→\n   168→const defaultSidecar = \"default-sidecar\"\n   169→\n   170→// DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace is a sidecar scope object with a default catch all egress listener\n   171→// that matches the default Istio behavior: a sidecar has listeners for all services in the mesh\n   172→// We use this scope when the user has not set any sidecar Config for a given config namespace.\n   173→func DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n   174→\tdefaultEgressListener := &IstioEgressListenerWrapper{\n   175→\t\tIstioListener: &networking.IstioEgressListener{\n   176→\t\t\tHosts: []string{\"*/*\"},\n   177→\t\t},\n   178→\t}\n   179→\tdefaultEgressListener.services = ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(configNamespace)\n   180→\tdefaultEgressListener.virtualServices = ps.VirtualServicesForGateway(configNamespace, constants.IstioMeshGateway)\n   181→\n   182→\tout := &SidecarScope{\n   183→\t\tName:               defaultSidecar,\n   184→\t\tNamespace:          configNamespace,\n   185→\t\tEgressListeners:    []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper{defaultEgressListener},\n   186→\t\tservices:           defaultEgressListener.services,\n   187→\t\tdestinationRules:   make(map[host.Name][]*config.Config),\n   188→\t\tservicesByHostname: make(map[host.Name]*Service, len(defaultEgressListener.services)),\n   189→\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n   190→\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n   191→\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n   192→\t}\n   193→\n   194→\t// Now that we have all the services that sidecars using this scope (in\n   195→\t// this config namespace) will see, identify all the destinationRules\n   196→\t// that these services need\n   197→\tfor _, s := range out.services {\n   198→\t\t// In some scenarios, there may be multiple Services defined for the same hostname due to ServiceEntry allowing\n   199→\t\t// arbitrary hostnames. In these cases, we want to pick the first Service, which is the oldest. This ensures\n   200→\t\t// newly created Services cannot take ownership unexpectedly.\n   201→\t\t// However, the Service is from Kubernetes it should take precedence over ones not. This prevents someone from\n   202→\t\t// \"domain squatting\" on the hostname before a Kubernetes Service is created.\n   203→\t\t// This relies on the assumption that\n   204→\t\tif existing, f := out.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname]; f &&\n   205→\t\t\t!(existing.Attributes.ServiceRegistry != provider.Kubernetes && s.Attributes.ServiceRegistry == provider.Kubernetes) {\n   206→\t\t\tcontinue\n   207→\t\t}\n   208→\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n   209→\t\tif dr := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); dr != nil {\n   210→\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = dr\n   211→\t\t}\n   212→\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   213→\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n   214→\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n   215→\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n   216→\t\t})\n   217→\t}\n   218→\n   219→\tfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n   220→\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n   221→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   222→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n   223→\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n   224→\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n   225→\t\t\t})\n   226→\t\t}\n   227→\t}\n   228→\n   229→\tfor _, el := range out.EgressListeners {\n   230→\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n   231→\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(el.virtualServices)\n   232→\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n   233→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n   234→\t\t}\n   235→\t\tfor _, vs := range el.virtualServices {\n   236→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   237→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n   238→\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n   239→\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n   240→\t\t\t})\n   241→\t\t}\n   242→\t}\n   243→\n   244→\tif ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy != nil {\n   245→\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = &networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy{\n   246→\t\t\tMode: networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n   247→\t\t}\n   248→\t}\n   249→\n   250→\treturn out\n   251→}\n   252→\n   253→// ConvertToSidecarScope converts from Sidecar config to SidecarScope object\n   254→func ConvertToSidecarScope(ps *PushContext, sidecarConfig *config.Config, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n   255→\tif sidecarConfig == nil {\n   256→\t\treturn DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, configNamespace)\n   257→\t}\n   258→\n   259→\tsidecar := sidecarConfig.Spec.(*networking.Sidecar)\n   260→\tout := &SidecarScope{\n   261→\t\tName:               sidecarConfig.Name,\n   262→\t\tNamespace:          configNamespace,\n   263→\t\tSidecar:            sidecar,\n   264→\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n   265→\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n   266→\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n   267→\t}\n   268→\n   269→\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   270→\t\tKind:      gvk.Sidecar,\n   271→\t\tName:      sidecarConfig.Name,\n   272→\t\tNamespace: sidecarConfig.Namespace,\n   273→\t})\n   274→\n   275→\tegressConfigs := sidecar.Egress\n   276→\t// If egress not set, setup a default listener\n   277→\tif len(egressConfigs) == 0 {\n   278→\t\tegressConfigs = append(egressConfigs, &networking.IstioEgressListener{Hosts: []string{\"*/*\"}})\n   279→\t}\n   280→\tout.EgressListeners = make([]*IstioEgressListenerWrapper, 0, len(egressConfigs))\n   281→\tfor _, e := range egressConfigs {\n   282→\t\tout.EgressListeners = append(out.EgressListeners,\n   283→\t\t\tconvertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps, configNamespace, e))\n   284→\t}\n   285→\n   286→\t// Now collect all the imported services across all egress listeners in\n   287→\t// this sidecar crd. This is needed to generate CDS output\n   288→\tout.services = make([]*Service, 0)\n   289→\ttype serviceIndex struct {\n   290→\t\tsvc   *Service\n   291→\t\tindex int // index record the position of the svc in slice\n   292→\t}\n   293→\tservicesAdded := make(map[host.Name]serviceIndex)\n   294→\taddService := func(s *Service) {\n   295→\t\tif s == nil {\n   296→\t\t\treturn\n   297→\t\t}\n   298→\t\tif foundSvc, found := servicesAdded[s.Hostname]; !found {\n   299→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   300→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n   301→\t\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n   302→\t\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n   303→\t\t\t})\n   304→\t\t\tout.services = append(out.services, s)\n   305→\t\t\tservicesAdded[s.Hostname] = serviceIndex{s, len(out.services) - 1}\n   306→\t\t} else if foundSvc.svc.Attributes.Namespace == s.Attributes.Namespace && s.Ports != nil && len(s.Ports) > 0 {\n   307→\t\t\t// merge the ports to service when each listener generates partial service\n   308→\t\t\t// we only merge if the found service is in the same namespace as the one we're trying to add\n   309→\t\t\tcopied := foundSvc.svc.DeepCopy()\n   310→\t\t\tfor _, p := range s.Ports {\n   311→\t\t\t\tfound := false\n   312→\t\t\t\tfor _, osp := range copied.Ports {\n   313→\t\t\t\t\tif p.Port == osp.Port {\n   314→\t\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n   315→\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   316→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   317→\t\t\t\t}\n   318→\t\t\t\tif !found {\n   319→\t\t\t\t\tcopied.Ports = append(copied.Ports, p)\n   320→\t\t\t\t}\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t\t// replace service in slice\n   323→\t\t\tout.services[foundSvc.index] = copied\n   324→\t\t}\n   325→\t}\n   326→\n   327→\tfor _, listener := range out.EgressListeners {\n   328→\t\t// First add the explicitly requested services, which take priority\n   329→\t\tfor _, s := range listener.services {\n   330→\t\t\taddService(s)\n   331→\t\t}\n   332→\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n   333→\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(listener.virtualServices)\n   334→\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n   335→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n   336→\t\t}\n   337→\n   338→\t\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(listener)\n   339→\t\t// Infer more possible destinations from virtual services\n   340→\t\t// Services chosen here will not override services explicitly requested in listener.services.\n   341→\t\t// That way, if there is ambiguity around what hostname to pick, a user can specify the one they\n   342→\t\t// want in the hosts field, and the potentially random choice below won't matter\n   343→\t\tfor _, vs := range listener.virtualServices {\n   344→\t\t\tv := vs.Spec.(*networking.VirtualService)\n   345→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   346→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n   347→\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n   348→\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n   349→\t\t\t})\n   350→\n   351→\t\t\tfor _, h := range virtualServiceDestinationHosts(v) {\n   352→\t\t\t\t// Default to this hostname in our config namespace\n   353→\t\t\t\tif s, ok := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)][configNamespace]; ok {\n   354→\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n   355→\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n   356→\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   357→\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(s, listener)\n   358→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   359→\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = s\n   360→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   361→\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n   362→\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n   363→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   364→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   365→\n   366→\t\t\t\t\t// We couldn't find the hostname in our config namespace\n   367→\t\t\t\t\t// We have to pick one arbitrarily for now, so we'll pick the first namespace alphabetically\n   368→\t\t\t\t\t// TODO: could we choose services more intelligently based on their ports?\n   369→\t\t\t\t\tbyNamespace := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)]\n   370→\t\t\t\t\tif len(byNamespace) == 0 {\n   371→\t\t\t\t\t\t// This hostname isn't found anywhere\n   372→\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Could not find service hostname %s parsed from %s\", h, vs.Key())\n   373→\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   374→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   375→\n   376→\t\t\t\t\tns := make([]string, 0, len(byNamespace))\n   377→\t\t\t\t\tfor k := range byNamespace {\n   378→\t\t\t\t\t\tif ps.IsServiceVisible(byNamespace[k], configNamespace) {\n   379→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tns = append(ns, k)\n   380→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   381→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   382→\t\t\t\t\tif len(ns) > 0 {\n   383→\t\t\t\t\t\tsort.Strings(ns)\n   384→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Pick first namespace alphabetically\n   385→\t\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n   386→\t\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n   387→\t\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   388→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(byNamespace[ns[0]], listener)\n   389→\t\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   390→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = byNamespace[ns[0]]\n   391→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   392→\t\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n   393→\t\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n   394→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   395→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   396→\t\t\t\t}\n   397→\t\t\t}\n   398→\t\t}\n   399→\t}\n   400→\n   401→\t// Now that we have all the services that sidecars using this scope (in\n   402→\t// this config namespace) will see, identify all the destinationRules\n   403→\t// that these services need\n   404→\tout.servicesByHostname = make(map[host.Name]*Service, len(out.services))\n   405→\tout.destinationRules = make(map[host.Name][]*config.Config)\n   406→\tfor _, s := range out.services {\n   407→\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n   408→\t\tif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n   409→\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n   410→\t\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n   411→\t\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   412→\t\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n   413→\t\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n   414→\t\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n   415→\t\t\t\t})\n   416→\t\t\t}\n   417→\t\t}\n   418→\t}\n   419→\n   420→\tif sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy == nil {\n   421→\t\tif ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy != nil {\n   422→\t\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = &networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy{\n   423→\t\t\t\tMode: networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n   424→\t\t\t}\n   425→\t\t}\n   426→\t} else {\n   427→\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n   428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\treturn out\n   431→}\n   432→\n   433→func convertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string,\n   434→\tistioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n   435→\tout := &IstioEgressListenerWrapper{\n   436→\t\tIstioListener: istioListener,\n   437→\t}\n   438→\n   439→\tout.listenerHosts = make(map[string][]host.Name)\n   440→\tfor _, h := range istioListener.Hosts {\n   441→\t\tparts := strings.SplitN(h, \"/\", 2)\n   442→\t\tif len(parts) < 2 {\n   443→\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"Illegal host in sidecar resource: %s, host must be of form namespace/dnsName\", h)\n   444→\t\t\tcontinue\n   445→\t\t}\n   446→\t\tif parts[0] == currentNamespace {\n   447→\t\t\tparts[0] = configNamespace\n   448→\t\t}\n   449→\t\tif _, exists := out.listenerHosts[parts[0]]; !exists {\n   450→\t\t\tout.listenerHosts[parts[0]] = make([]host.Name, 0)\n   451→\t\t}\n   452→\t\tout.listenerHosts[parts[0]] = append(out.listenerHosts[parts[0]], host.Name(parts[1]))\n   453→\t}\n   454→\n   455→\tvses := ps.VirtualServicesForGateway(configNamespace, constants.IstioMeshGateway)\n   456→\tout.virtualServices = SelectVirtualServices(vses, out.listenerHosts)\n   457→\tsvces := ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(configNamespace)\n   458→\tout.services = out.selectServices(svces, configNamespace, out.listenerHosts)\n   459→\n   460→\treturn out\n   461→}\n   462→\n   463→// GetEgressListenerForRDS returns the egress listener corresponding to\n   464→// the listener port or the bind address or the catch all listener\n   465→func (sc *SidecarScope) GetEgressListenerForRDS(port int, bind string) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n   466→\tif sc == nil {\n   467→\t\treturn nil\n   468→\t}\n   469→\n   470→\tfor _, e := range sc.EgressListeners {\n   471→\t\t// We hit a catchall listener. This is the last listener in the list of listeners\n   472→\t\t// return as is\n   473→\t\tif e.IstioListener == nil || e.IstioListener.Port == nil {\n   474→\t\t\treturn e\n   475→\t\t}\n   476→\n   477→\t\t// Check if the ports match\n   478→\t\t// for unix domain sockets (i.e. port == 0), check if the bind is equal to the routeName\n   479→\t\tif int(e.IstioListener.Port.Number) == port {\n   480→\t\t\tif port == 0 { // unix domain socket\n   481→\t\t\t\tif e.IstioListener.Bind == bind {\n   482→\t\t\t\t\treturn e\n   483→\t\t\t\t}\n   484→\t\t\t\t// no match.. continue searching\n   485→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   486→\t\t\t}\n   487→\t\t\t// this is a non-zero port match\n   488→\t\t\treturn e\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\t// This should never be reached unless user explicitly set an empty array for egress\n   493→\t// listeners which we actually forbid\n   494→\treturn nil\n   495→}\n   496→\n   497→// HasIngressListener returns if the sidecar scope has ingress 538→\t_, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n   539→\treturn exists\n   540→}\n   541→\n   542→// AddConfigDependencies add extra config dependencies to this scope. This action should be done before the\n   543→// SidecarScope being used to avoid concurrent read/write.\n   544→func (sc *SidecarScope) AddConfigDependencies(dependencies ...ConfigKey) {\n   545→\tif *SidecarScope) DestinationRule(direction TrafficDirection, proxy *Proxy, svc host.Name) *config.Config {\n   559→\tdestinationRules := sc.destinationRules[svc]\n   560→\tvar catchAllDr *config.Config\n   561→\tfor _, destRule := range destinationRules {\n   562→\t\tdestinationRule := destRule.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n   563→\t\tif destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == destRule.Namespace &&\n   570→\t\t\tdestinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil && direction == TrafficDirectionOutbound {\n   571→\t\t\tworkloadLabels := labels.Collection{proxy.Metadata.Labels}\n   572→\t\t\tworkloadSelector := labels.Instance(destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector().GetMatchLabels())\n   573→\t\t\t// return destination rule if workload selector matches\n   574→\t\t\tif portion of the Sidecar config.\n   592→// Note that the returned service could be trimmed.\n   593→func (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) selectServices(services []*Service, configNamespace string, hosts map[string][]host.Name) []*Service {\n   594→\timportedServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   595→\twildcardHosts, wnsFound := hosts[wildcardNamespace]\n   596→\tfor _, s := range services {\n   597→\t\tconfigNamespace := s.Attributes.Namespace\n   598→\n   599→\t\t// Check if there is an explicit import of form ns/* or ns/host\n   600→\t\tif importedHosts, nsFound := hosts[configNamespace]; // Check if there is an import of form */host or */*\n   605→\t\t\tif svc := matchingService(wildcardHosts, s, ilw); svc != nil {\n   606→\t\t\t\timportedServices = append(importedServices, svc)\n   607→\t\t\t}\n   608→\t\t}\n   609→\t}\n   610→\n   611→\tvalidServices := make(map[host.Name]string)\n   612→\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n   613→\t\t_, f := validServices[svc.Hostname]\n 619→\t\t}\n   620→\t}\n   621→\n   622→\tfilteredServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   623→\t// Filter down to just instances in scope for the service\n   624→\tfor _, svc := range importedServices {\n   625→\t\tif validServices[svc.Hostname] == svc.Attributes.Namespace {\n   626→\t\t\tfilteredServices = append(filteredServices, svc)\n   627→\t\t}\n   628→\t}\n   629→\treturn filteredServices\n   630→}\n   631→\n   632→// Return the original service or a trimmed service which has a subset of the ports in original service.\n   633→func matchingService(importedHosts []host.Name, service *Service, ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) *Service {\n   634→\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(ilw)\n   635→\tfor _, importedHost := range importedHosts {\n   636→\t\t// Check if the hostnames match per usual hostname matching rules\n   637→\t\tif service.Hostname.SubsetOf(importedHost) {\n   638→\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   639→\t\t\t\treturn serviceMatchingListenerPort(service, ilw)\n   640→\t\t\t}\n   641→\t\t\treturn service\n   642→\t\t}\n   643→\t}\n   644→\treturn nil\n   645→}\n   646→\n   647→// serviceMatchingListenerPort constructs service with listener port.\n   648→func serviceMatchingListenerPort(service *Service, ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) *Service {\n   649→\tfor _, port := range service.Ports {\n   650→\t\tif port.Port == int(ilw.IstioListener.Port.GetNumber()) {\n   651→\t\t\tsc := service.DeepCopy()\n   652→\t\t\tsc.Ports = []*Port{port}\n   653→\t\t\treturn sc\n   654→\t\t}\n   655→\t}\n   656→\treturn nil\n   657→}\n   658→\n   659→func needsPortMatch(ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) bool {\n   660→\t// If a listener is defined with a port, we should match services with port except in the following case.\n   661→\t//  - If Port's protocol is proxy protocol(HTTP_PROXY) in which case the egress listener is used as generic egress http proxy.\n   662→\treturn ilw.IstioListener != nil && ilw.IstioListener.Port.GetNumber() != 0 &&\n   663→\t\tprotocol.Parse(ilw.IstioListener.Port.Protocol) != protocol.HTTP_PROXY\n   664→}\n   665→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you Sidecar resource with some\n// preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\n// and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n// sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n// list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n// SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n// services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n// wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n// settings.\n//\n// Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n// SidecarScope object. If the proxy's namespace does not have a user\n// specified Sidecar CRD, we will construct one that has a catch all egress\n// listener that imports every public service/virtualService in the mesh.\ntype SidecarScope struct {\n\tName string\n\t// This is the namespace where the sidecar takes effect,\n\t// maybe different from the ns where sidecar resides if sidecar is in root ns.\n\tNamespace string\n\t// The crd itself. Can be nil if we are constructing the default\n\t// sidecar scope\n\tSidecar *networking.Sidecar\n\n\t// Version this sidecar was computed for\n\tVersion string\n\n\t// Set of egress listeners, and their associated services.  A sidecar\n\t// scope should have either ingress/egress listeners or both.  For\n\t// every proxy workload that maps to a sidecar API object (or the\n\t// default object), we will go through every egress listener in the\n\t// object and process the Envoy listener or RDS based on the imported\n\t// services/virtual services in that listener.\n\tEgressListeners []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper\n\n\t// Union of services imported across all egress listeners for use by CDS code.\n\tservices           []*Service\n\tservicesByHostname map[host.Name]*Service\n\n\t// Destination rules imported across all egress listeners. This\n\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\n\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\n\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\n\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\n\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\n\t// destination rule.\n\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\n\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\n\t// be forwarded.\n\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n\n\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\n\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\n\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\n\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\n\n\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\n\t// Istio configuration.\n\t//\n\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\n\tRootNamespace string\n}\n\n// MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\n\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\n\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"version\":               sc.Version,\n\t\t\"rootNamespace\":         sc.RootNamespace,\n\t\t\"name\":                  sc.Name,\n\t\t\"namespace\":             sc.Namespace,\n\t\t\"outboundTrafficPolicy\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\n\t\t\"services\":              sc.services,\n\t\t\"sidecar\":               sc.Sidecar,\n\t\t\"destinationRules\":      sc.destinationRules,\n\t}, \"\", \"  \")\n}\n\n// IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\n// networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\n// optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\n// services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\ntype IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\n\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\n\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\n\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\n\n\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\n\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\n\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\n\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\n\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\n\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\n\tservices []*Service\n\n\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// As with per listener services, this\n\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\n\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\n\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. We need a\n\t// virtualService set per listener and not one per sidecarScope because\n\t// each listener imports an independent set of virtual services.\n\t// Listener 1 could import a public virtual service for serviceA from\n\t// namespace A that has some path rewrite, while listener2 could import\n\t// a private virtual service for serviceA from the local namespace,\n\t// with a different path rewrite or no path rewrites.\n\tvirtualServices []config.Config\n\n\tlistenerHosts map[string][]host.Name\n}\n\nconst defaultSidecar = \"default-sidecar\"\n\n// DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace is a sidecar scope object with a default catch all egress listener\n// that matches the default Istio behavior: a sidecar has listeners for all services in the mesh\n// We use this scope when the user has not set any sidecar Config for a given config namespace.\nfunc DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n\tdefaultEgressListener := networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn out\n}\n\n// ConvertToSidecarScope converts from Sidecar config to SidecarScope object\nfunc configNamespace)\n\t}\n\n\tsidecar := sidecarConfig.Spec.(*networking.Sidecar)\n\tout := &SidecarScope{\n\t\tName:               sidecarConfig.Name,\n\t\tNamespace: {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n\t\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n\t\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\tout.services = ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(listener.virtualServices)\n\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(listener)\n\t\t// Infer more possible destinations from virtual services\n\t\t// Services chosen here will not override services explicitly requested in listener.services.\n\t\t// That for example each K8S cluster is a registry\n   260→// instance. Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\n   261→// of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\n   262→// A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\n   263→// deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\n   264→// to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\n   265→// or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\n   266→// scalability.\n   267→//\n   268→// Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\n   269→// reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. This design assumes pilot\n   270→// tracks all endpoints in the mesh and they fit in RAM - so limit is few M endpoints.\n   271→// It is possible to split the endpoint tracking in future.\n   272→type XDSUpdater interface {\n   273→\t// EDSUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n   274→\t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n   275→\t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n   276→\t// registry name.\n   277→\tEDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n   278→\n   279→\t// EDSCacheUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n   280→\t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n   281→\t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n   282→\t// registry name.\n   283→\t// Note: the difference with `EDSUpdate` is that it only update the cache rather than requesting a push\n   284→\tEDSCacheUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n   285→\n   286→\t// SvcUpdate is called when a service definition is updated/deleted.\n   287→\tSvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event Event)\n   288→\n   289→\t// ConfigUpdate is called to notify the XDS server of config updates and request a push.\n   290→\t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n   291→\tConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n   292→\n   293→\t// ProxyUpdate is called to notify the XDS server to send a push to the specified proxy.\n   294→\t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n   295→\tProxyUpdate(clusterID cluster.ID, ip string)\n   296→\n   297→\t// RemoveShard removes all endpoints for the given shard key\n   298→\tRemoveShard(shardKey ShardKey)\n   299→}\n   300→\n   301→// shardRegistry is a simplified interface for registries that can produce a shard key\n   302→type shardRegistry interface {\n   303→\tCluster() cluster.ID\n   304→\tProvider() provider.ID\n   305→}\n   306→\n   307→func NewShardKey(cluster cluster.ID, provider provider.ID) ShardKey {\n   308→\treturn to the config update debouncer and pass to the PushQueue.\n   329→type PushRequest struct {\n   330→\t// Full determines whether a full push is required or not. If false, an incremental update will be sent.\n   331→\t// Incremental pushes:\n   332→\t// * Do not recompute the push context\n   333→\t// * Do not recompute proxy state (such as ServiceInstances)\n   334→\t// * Are not reported in standard metrics such as push time\n   335→\t// As a result, configuration updates should never be incremental. Generally, only EDS will set this, but\n   336→\t// in the future SDS will as well.\n   337→\tFull bool\n   338→\n   339→\t// ConfigsUpdated keeps track of configs that have changed.\n   340→\t// This is used as an optimization to avoid unnecessary pushes to proxies that are scoped with a Sidecar.\n   341→\t// If this is empty, then all proxies will get an update.\n   342→\t// Otherwise only proxies depend on these configs will get an update.\n   343→\t// The kind of resources are defined in pkg/config/schemas.\n   344→\tConfigsUpdated map[ConfigKey]struct{}\n   345→\n   346→\t// Push stores the push context to use for the update. This may initially be nil, as we will\n   347→\t// debounce changes before a PushContext is eventually created.\n   348→\tPush *PushContext\n   349→\n   350→\t// Start represents the time a push was started. This represents the time of adding to the PushQueue.\n   351→\t// Note that this does not include time spent debouncing.\n   352→\tStart time.Time\n   353→\n   354→\t// Reason represents the reason for requesting a push. This should only be a fixed set of values,\n   355→\t// to avoid unbounded cardinality in metrics. If this is not set, it may be automatically filled in later.\n   356→\t// There should only be multiple reasons if the push request is the result of two distinct triggers, rather than\n   357→\t// classifying a single trigger as having multiple reasons.\n   358→\tReason []TriggerReason\n   359→\n   360→\t// Delta defines the resources that were added or removed as part of this push request.\n   361→\t// This is set only on requests from the client which change the set of resources they (un)subscribe from.\n   362→\tDelta ResourceDelta\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→// ResourceDelta records the difference in requested resources by an XDS client\n   366→type ResourceDelta struct {\n   367→\t// Subscribed indicates the client requested these additional resources\n   368→\tSubscribed sets.Set\n   369→\t// Unsubscribed indicates the client no longer requires these resources\n   370→\tUnsubscribed sets.Set\n   371→}\n   372→\n   373→func (rd ResourceDelta) IsEmpty() bool {\n   374→\treturn len(rd.Subscribed) == 0 && len(rd.Unsubscribed) == 0\n   375→}\n   376→\n   377→type TriggerReason string\n   378→\n   379→// If adding a new reason, update xds/monitoring.go:triggerMetric\n   380→const (\n   381→\t// EndpointUpdate describes a push triggered by an Endpoint change\n   382→\tEndpointUpdate TriggerReason = \"endpoint\"\n   383→\t// ConfigUpdate describes a push triggered by a NamespaceUpdate describes a push triggered by a Namespace change\n   402→\tNamespaceUpdate TriggerReason = \"namespace\"\n   403→\t// ClusterUpdate describes a push triggered by a Cluster change\n   404→\tClusterUpdate TriggerReason = \"cluster\"\n   405→)\n   406→\n   407→// Merge two update requests together\n   408→// Merge behaves similarly to a list append; usage should in the form `a = a.merge(b)`.\n   409→// Importantly, Merge may decide to allocate a new PushRequest object or reuse the existing one - both\n   410→// inputs should not be used after completion.\n   411→func (pr *PushRequest) Merge(other *PushRequest) *PushRequest {\n   412→\tif pr == nil {\n   413→\t\treturn other\n   414→\t}\n   415→\tif other == nil {\n   416→\t\treturn pr\n   417→\t}\n   418→\n   419→\t// Keep the first (older) start time\n   420→\n   421→\t// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count\n   422→\tpr.Reason = append(pr.Reason, other.Reason...)\n   423→\n   424→\t// If either is full we need a full push\n   425→\tpr.Full = pr.Full || other.Full\n   426→\n   427→\t// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date\n   428→\tif other.Push != nil {\n   429→\t\tpr.Push = other.Push\n   430→\t}\n   431→\n   432→\t// Do not merge when any one is empty\n   433→\tif len(pr.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 || len(other.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 {\n   434→\t\tpr.ConfigsUpdated = nil\n   435→\t} else {\n   436→\t\tfor conf := range other.ConfigsUpdated {\n   437→\t\t\tpr.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n   438→\t\t}\n   439→\t}\n   440→\n   441→\treturn pr\n   442→}\n   443→\n   444→// CopyMerge two update requests together. Unlike Merge, this will not mutate either input.\n   445→// This should be used when we are modifying a shared PushRequest (typically any time it's in the context\n   446→// of a single proxy)\n   447→func (pr *PushRequest) CopyMerge(other *PushRequest) *PushRequest {\n   448→\tif pr == nil {\n   449→\t\treturn other\n   450→\t}\n   451→\tif other == nil {\n   452→\t\treturn pr\n   453→\t}\n   454→\n   455→\tvar reason []TriggerReason\n   456→\tif len(pr.Reason)+len(other.Reason) > 0 {\n   457→\t\treason = make([]TriggerReason, 0, len(pr.Reason)+len(other.Reason))\n   458→\t\treason = append(reason, pr.Reason...)\n   459→\t\treason = append(reason, other.Reason...)\n   460→\t}\n   461→\tmerged := &PushRequest{\n   462→\t\t// Keep the first (older) start time\n   463→\t\tStart: pr.Start,\n   464→\n   465→\t\t// If either is full we need a full push\n   466→\t\tFull: pr.Full || other.Full,\n   467→\n   468→\t\t// The other push context is presumed to be later and more up to date\n   469→\t\tPush: other.Push,\n   470→\n   471→\t\t// Merge the two reasons. Note that we shouldn't deduplicate here, or we would under count\n   472→\t\tReason: reason,\n   473→\t}\n   474→\n   475→\t// Do not merge when any one is empty\n   476→\tif len(pr.ConfigsUpdated) > 0 && len(other.ConfigsUpdated) > 0 {\n   477→\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated = make(map[ConfigKey]struct{}, len(pr.ConfigsUpdated)+len(other.ConfigsUpdated))\n   478→\t\tfor conf := range pr.ConfigsUpdated {\n   479→\t\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n   480→\t\t}\n   481→\t\tfor conf := range other.ConfigsUpdated {\n   482→\t\t\tmerged.ConfigsUpdated[conf] = struct{}{}\n   483→\t\t}\n   484→\t}\n   485→\n   486→\treturn merged\n   487→}\n   488→\n   489→func (pr *PushRequest) PushReason() string {\n   490→\tif len(pr.Reason) == 1 && pr.Reason[0] == ProxyRequest {\n   491→\t\treturn \" request\"\n   492→\t}\n   493→\treturn \"\"\n   494→}\n   495→\n   496→// ProxyPushStatus represents an event captured during config push to proxies.\n   497→// It may contain additional message and the affected proxy.\n   498→type ProxyPushStatus struct {\n   499→\tProxy   string `json:\"proxy,omitempty\"`\n   500→\tMessage string `json:\"message,omitempty\"`\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\n// of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\n// A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\n// deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\n// to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\n// or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\n// scalability.\n//\n// Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\n// reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. This design assumes pilot\n// tracks all endpoints in the mesh and they fit in RAM - so limit is few M endpoints.\n// It is possible to split the endpoint tracking in future.\ntype XDSUpdater interface {\n\t// EDSUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\n\t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\n\t// must be sent. The shard name is used as a key - current implementation is using the\n\t// registry name.\n\t// Note: the difference with `EDSUpdate` is that it only update the cache rather than requesting a push\n\tEDSCacheUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, entry []*IstioEndpoint)\n\n\t// SvcUpdate is called when a service definition is updated/deleted.\n\tSvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, namespace string, event Event)\n\n\t// ConfigUpdate is called to notify the XDS server of config updates and request a push.\n\t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n\tConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n\n\t// ProxyUpdate is called to notify the XDS server to send a push to the specified proxy.\n\t// The requests may be collapsed and throttled.\n\tProxyUpdate(clusterID cluster.ID, ip string)\n\n\t// RemoveShard removes all endpoints for the given shard key\n\tRemoveShard(shardKey ShardKey)\n}\n\n// shardRegistry is a simplified interface for registries that can produce a shard key\ntype shardRegistry interface {\n\tCluster() cluster.ID\n\tProvider() provider.ID\n}\n\nfunc NewShardKey(cluster cluster.ID, provider provider.ID) ShardKey {\n\treturn ShardKey(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", cluster, provider))\n}\n\n// ShardKeyFromRegistry computes the shard key based on provider type and cluster id.\nfunc ShardKeyFromRegistry(instance shardRegistry) ShardKey {\n\treturn NewShardKey(instance.Cluster(), instance.Provider())\n}\n\n// ShardKey is the key for EndpointShards made of a key with the format \"cluster/provider\"\ntype ShardKey string\n\nfunc (sk ShardKey) Cluster() cluster.ID {\n\tp := strings.Split(string(sk), \"/\")\n\tif len(p) < 1 {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\treturn cluster.ID(p[0])\n}\n\n// PushRequest defines a request to push to proxies\n// It is used to send updates to the config update debouncer and pass to the PushQueue.\ntype PushRequest struct {\n\t// Full determines whether a full push is required or not.  1043→\t\t\treturn out\n  1044→\t\t}\n  1045→\t}\n  1046→\n  1047→\t// 4. if no public/private rule in calling proxy's namespace matched, and no public rule in the\n  1048→\t// target service's namespace matched, search for any exported destination rule in the config root namespace\n  1049→\tif out := ps.getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(ps.Mesh.RootNamespace, service.Hostname, proxyNameSpace); out != nil {\n  1050→\t\treturn out\n  1051→\t}\n  1052→\n  1053→\t// 5. service DestinationRules were merged in SetDestinationRules, return mesh/namespace rules if present\n  1054→\tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance {\n  1055→\t\t// return namespace rule if present\n  1056→\t\tif out := ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[proxyNameSpace]; out != nil {\n  1057→\t\t\treturn []*config.Config{out}\n  1058→\t\t}\n  1059→\t\t// return mesh rule\n  1060→\t\tif out := ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[ps.Mesh.RootNamespace]; out != nil {\n  1061→\t\t\treturn []*config.Config{out}\n  1062→\t\t}\n  1063→\t}\n  1064→\n  1065→\treturn nil\n  1066→}\n  1067→\n  1068→func (ps *PushContext) getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace(owningNamespace string, hostname host.Name, clientNamespace string) []*config.Config {\n  1069→\tif ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace] != nil {\n  1070→\t\tif specificHostname, ok := MostSpecificHostMatch(hostname,\n  1071→\t\t\tps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].destRules,\n  1072→\t\t); ok {\n  1073→\t\t\t// Check if the dest rule for this host is actually exported to the proxy's (client) namespace\n  1074→\t\t\texportToMap := ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].exportTo[specificHostname]\n  1075→\t\t\tif len(exportToMap) == 0 || exportToMap[visibility.Public] || exportToMap[visibility.Instance(clientNamespace)] {\n  1076→\t\t\t\tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance {\n  1077→\t\t\t\t\tvar parent *config.Config\n  1078→\t\t\t\t\t// client inherits global DR from its own namespace, not from the exported DR's owning namespace\n  1079→\t\t\t\t\t// grab the client namespace DR or mesh if none exists\n  1080→\t\t\t\t\tif parent = ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[clientNamespace]; parent == nil {\n  1081→\t\t\t\t\t\tparent = ps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace[ps.Mesh.RootNamespace]\n  1082→\t\t\t\t\t}\n  1083→\t\t\t\t\tvar inheritedDrList []*config.Config\n  1084→\t\t\t\t\tfor _, child := range ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].destRules[specificHostname] {\n  1085→\t\t\t\t\t\tinheritedDr := ps.inheritDestinationRule(parent, child)\n  1086→\t\t\t\t\t\tif inheritedDr != nil {\n  1087→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinheritedDrList = append(inheritedDrList, inheritedDr)\n  1088→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n  1089→\n  1090→\t\t\t\t\t}\n  1091→\t\t\t\t\treturn inheritedDrList\n  1092→\t\t\t\t}\n  1093→\t\t\t\tif dr, ok := ps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace[owningNamespace].destRules[specificHostname]; ok {\n  1094→\t\t\t\t\treturn dr\n  1095→\t\t\t\t}\n  1096→\t\t\t}\n  1097→\t\t}\n  1098→\t}\n  1099→\treturn nil\n  1100→}\n  1101→\n  1102→// IsClusterLocal indicates whether the endpoints for the service should only be accessible to clients\n  1103→// within the cluster.\n  1104→func (ps *PushContext) IsClusterLocal(service *Service) bool {\n  1105→\tif service == nil {\n  1106→\t\treturn false\n  1107→\t}\n  1108→\treturn ps.clusterLocalHosts.IsClusterLocal(service.Hostname)\n  1109→}\n  1110→\n  1111→// InitContext will initialize the data structures used for code generation.\n  1112→// This should be called before starting the push, from the thread creating\n  1113→// the push context.\n  1114→func (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) error {\n  1115→\t// Acquire a lock to ensure we don't concurrently initialize the same PushContext.\n  1116→\t// If this does happen, one thread will block then exit early from InitDone=true\n  1117→\tps.initializeMutex.Lock()\n  1118→\tdefer ps.initializeMutex.Unlock()\n  1119→\tif ps.InitDone.Load() {\n  1120→\t\treturn nil\n  1121→\t}\n  1122→\n  1123→\tps.Mesh = env.Mesh()\n  1124→\tps.LedgerVersion = env.Version()\n  1125→\n  1126→\t// Must be initialized first\n  1127→\t// as initServiceRegistry/VirtualServices/Destrules\n  1128→\t// use the default export map\n  1129→\tps.initDefaultExportMaps()\n  1130→\n  1131→\t// create new or incremental update\n  1132→\tif pushReq == nil || oldPushContext == nil || !oldPushContext.InitDone.Load() || len(pushReq.ConfigsUpdated) == 0 {\n  1133→\t\tif err := ps.createNewContext(env); err != nil {\n  1134→\t\t\treturn err\n  1135→\t\t}\n  1136→\t} else {\n  1137→\t\tif err := ps.updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq); err != nil {\n  1138→\t\t\treturn err\n  1139→\t\t}\n  1140→\t}\n  1141→\n  1142→\tps.networkMgr = env.NetworkManager\n  1143→\n  1144→\tps.clusterLocalHosts = env.ClusterLocal().GetClusterLocalHosts()\n  1145→\n  1146→\tps.InitDone.Store(true)\n  1147→\treturn nil\n  1148→}\n  1149→\n  1150→func (ps *PushContext) createNewContext(env *Environment) error {\n  1151→\tif err := ps.initServiceRegistry(env); err != nil {\n  1152→\t\treturn err\n  1153→\t}\n  1154→\n  1155→\tif err :=  1170→\n  1171→\tif err := ps.initAuthorizationPolicies(env); err != nil {\n  1172→\t\tauthzLog.Errorf(\"failed to initialize authorization policies: %v\", err)\n  1173→\t\treturn err\n  1174→\t}\n 1182→\t}\n  1183→\n  1184→\tif err := ps.initWasmPlugins(env); err != nil {\n  1185→\t\treturn err\n  1186→\t}\n  1187→\n  1188→\tif err := ps.initEnvoyFilters(env); err != nil {\n  1189→\t\treturn 1205→\toldPushContext *PushContext,\n  1206→\tpushReq *PushRequest) error {\n  1207→\tvar servicesChanged, virtualServicesChanged, destinationRulesChanged, gatewayChanged,\n  1208→\t\tauthnChanged, authzChanged, envoyFiltersChanged, sidecarsChanged, telemetryChanged, gatewayAPIChanged,\n  1209→\t\twasmPluginsChanged, proxyConfigsChanged bool\n  1210→\n  1211→\tfor conf := range registry, and creates a map\n  1349→// of hostname to service\n  1350→func (ps *PushContext) initServiceRegistry(env *Environment) error {\n  1351→\t// Sort the services in order of creation.\n  1352→\tallServices := SortServicesByCreationTime(env.Services())\n  1353→\tfor _, s := range allServices {\n  1354→\t\tsvcKey := s.Key()\n  1355→\t\t// Precache instances\n  1356→\t\tfor _, port := 1360→\t\t\tinstances := make([]*ServiceInstance, 0)\n  1361→\t\t\tinstances = append(instances, env.InstancesByPort(s, port.Port, nil)...)\n  1362→\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.instancesByPort[svcKey][port.Port] = instances\n  1363→\t\t}\n  1364→\n  1365→\t\tif _, f := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[s.Hostname]; !f {\n  1366→\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[s.Hostname] = map[string]*Service{}\n  1367→\t\t}\n  1368→\t\tps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[s.Hostname][s.Attributes.Namespace] = s\n  1369→\n  1370→\t\tns := s.Attributes.Namespace\n  1371→\t\tif len(s.Attributes.ExportTo) == 0 {\n  1372→\t\t\tif ps.exportToDefaults.service[visibility.Private] {\n  1373→\t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.privateByNamespace[ns] = append(ps.ServiceIndex.privateByNamespace[ns], s)\n  1374→\t\t\t} else if ps.exportToDefaults.service[visibility.Public] {\n  1375→\t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.public = append(ps.ServiceIndex.public, s)\n  1376→\t\t\t}\n  1377→\t\t} else {\n  1378→\t\t\t// if service has exportTo ~ - i.e. not visible to anyone, ignore all exportTos\n  1379→\t\t\t// if service has exportTo *, make public and ignore all other exportTos\n  1380→\t\t\t// if service has exportTo ., replace with current namespace\n  1381→\t\t\tif s.Attributes.ExportTo[visibility.Public] {\n  1382→\t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.public = append(ps.ServiceIndex.public, s)\n  1383→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1384→\t\t\t} else if s.Attributes.ExportTo[visibility.None] {\n  1385→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1386→\t\t\t} else {\n  1387→\t\t\t\t// . or other namespaces\n  1388→\t\t\t\tfor exportTo := range s.Attributes.ExportTo {\n  1389→\t\t\t\t\tif exportTo == visibility.Private || string(exportTo) == ns {\n  1390→\t\t\t\t\t\t// exportTo with same namespace is effectively private\n  1391→\t\t\t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.privateByNamespace[ns] = append(ps.ServiceIndex.privateByNamespace[ns], s)\n  1392→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n  1393→\t\t\t\t\t\t// exportTo is a specific target namespace\n  1394→\t\t\t\t\t\tps.ServiceIndex.exportedToNamespace[string(exportTo)] = append(ps.ServiceIndex.exportedToNamespace[string(exportTo)], s)\n  1395→\t\t\t\t\t}\n  1396→\t\t\t\t}\n  1397→\t\t\t}\n  1398→\t\t}\n  1399→\t}\n  1400→\n  1401→\tps.initServiceAccounts(env, allServices)\n  1402→\n  1403→\treturn nil\n  1404→}\n  1405→\n  1406→// SortServicesByCreationTime sorts the list of services in ascending order by their creation time (if available).\n  1407→func SortServicesByCreationTime(services []*Service) []*Service {\n  1408→\tsort.SliceStable(services, func(i, j int) bool {\n  1409→\t\t// If creation time is the same, then behavior is nondeterministic. In this case, we can\n  1410→\t\t// pick an arbitrary but consistent ordering based on name and namespace, which is unique.\n  1411→\t\t// CreationTimestamp is stored in seconds, so this is not uncommon.\n  1412→\t\tif services[i].CreationTime.Equal(services[j].CreationTime) {\n  1413→\t\t\tin := services[i].Attributes.Name + \".\" + services[i].Attributes.Namespace\n  1414→\t\t\tjn := services[j].Attributes.Name + \".\" + services[j].Attributes.Namespace\n  1415→\t\t\treturn in < jn\n  1416→\t\t}\n  1417→\t\treturn services[i].CreationTime.Before(services[j].CreationTime)\n  1418→\t})\n  1419→\treturn services\n  1420→}\n  1421→\n  1422→// Caches list of service accounts in the registry\n  1423→func (ps *PushContext) initServiceAccounts(env *Environment, services []*Service) {\n  1424→\tfor _, svc := range services {\n  1425→\t\tif ps.ServiceAccounts[svc.Hostname] == nil {\n  1426→\t\t\tps.ServiceAccounts[svc.Hostname] = map[int][]string{}\n  1427→\t\t}\n  1428→\t\tfor _, port := range svc.Ports {\n  1429→\t\t\tif port.Protocol == protocol.UDP {\n  1430→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1431→\t\t\t}\n  1432→\t\t\tps.ServiceAccounts[svc.Hostname][port.Port] = env.GetIstioServiceAccounts(svc, []int{port.Port})\n  1433→\t\t}\n  1434→\t}\n  1435→}\n  1436→\n  1437→// Caches list of authentication policies\n  1438→func (ps *PushContext) initAuthnPolicies(env list of virtual services\n  1446→func (ps *PushContext) initVirtualServices(env *Environment) error {\n  1447→\tps.virtualServiceIndex.exportedToNamespaceByGateway = sidecarConfig.Namespace))\n  1633→\t\tif rootNSConfig == nil && sidecarConfig.Namespace == ps.Mesh.RootNamespace &&\n  1634→\t\t\tsidecarConfig.Spec.(*networking.Sidecar).WorkloadSelector == nil {\n  1635→\t\t\trootNSConfig = &sidecarConfigs[i]\n  1636→\t\t}\n  1637→\t}\n  1638→\tps.sidecarIndex.rootConfig = rootNSConfig\n  1639→\n  1640→\treturn nil\n  1641→}\n  1642→\n  1643→// Split out of DestinationRule expensive conversions - once per push.\n  1644→func (ps *PushContext) initDestinationRules(env *Environment) error {\n  1645→\tconfigs, err := env.List(gvk.DestinationRule, NamespaceAll)\n  1646→\tif err != nil {\n  1647→\t\treturn err\n  1648→\t}\n  1649→\n  1650→\t// values returned from ConfigStore.List are immutable.\n  1651→\t// Therefore, we make a copy\n  1652→\tdestRules := make([]config.Config, len(configs))\n  1653→\tfor i := range destRules {\n  1654→\t\tdestRules[i] = configs[i].DeepCopy()\n  1655→\t}\n  1656→\n  1657→\tps.SetDestinationRules(destRules)\n  1658→\treturn nil\n  1659→}\n  1660→\n  1661→func newProcessedDestRules() *consolidatedDestRules {\n  1662→\treturn &consolidatedDestRules{\n  1663→\t\texportTo:  map[host.Name]map[visibility.Instance]bool{},\n  1664→\t\tdestRules: map[host.Name][]*config.Config{},\n  1665→\t}\n  1666→}\n  1667→\n  1668→// SetDestinationRules is updates internal structures using a set of configs.\n  1669→// Split out of DestinationRule expensive conversions, computed once per push.\n  1670→// This also allows tests to inject a config without having the mock.\n  1671→// This will not work properly for Sidecars, which will precompute their destination rules on init\n  1672→func (ps *PushContext) SetDestinationRules(configs []config.Config) {\n  1673→\t// Sort by time first. So if two destination rule have top level traffic policies\n  1674→\t// we take the first one.\n  1675→\tsortConfigByCreationTime(configs)\n  1676→\tnamespaceLocalDestRules := make(map[string]*consolidatedDestRules)\n  1677→\texportedDestRulesByNamespace := make(map[string]*consolidatedDestRules)\n  1678→\trootNamespaceLocalDestRules := newProcessedDestRules()\n  1679→\tinheritedConfigs := make(map[string]*config.Config)\n  1680→\n  1681→\tfor i := range configs {\n  1682→\t\trule := configs[i].Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n  1683→\n  1684→\t\tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance && rule.Host == \"\" {\n  1685→\t\t\tif t, ok := inheritedConfigs[configs[i].Namespace]; ok {\n  1686→\t\t\t\tlog.Warnf(\n  1687→\t\t\t\t\t\"Namespace/mesh-level DestinationRule is already defined for %q at time %v. Ignore %q which was created at time %v\",\n  1688→\t\t\t\t\tconfigs[i].Namespace, t.CreationTimestamp, configs[i].Name, configs[i].CreationTimestamp)\n  1689→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1690→\t\t\t}\n  1691→\t\t\tinheritedConfigs[configs[i].Namespace] = &configs[i]\n  1692→\t\t}\n  1693→\n  1694→\t\trule.Host = string(ResolveShortnameToFQDN(rule.Host, configs[i].Meta))\n  1695→\t\texportToMap := make(map[visibility.Instance]bool)\n  1696→\n  1697→\t\t// destination rules with workloadSelector should not be exported to other namespaces\n  1698→\t\tif rule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil {\n  1699→\t\t\tfor _, e := range rule.ExportTo {\n  1700→\t\t\t\texportToMap[visibility.Instance(e)] = true\n  1701→\t\t\t}\n  1702→\t\t}\n  1703→\n  1704→\t\t// add only if the dest rule is exported with . or * or explicit exportTo containing this namespace\n  1705→\t\t// The global exportTo doesn't matter here (its either . or * - both of which are applicable here)\n  1706→\t\tif len(exportToMap) == 0 || exportToMap[visibility.Public] || exportToMap[visibility.Private] ||\n  1707→\t\t\texportToMap[visibility.Instance(configs[i].Namespace)] {\n  1708→\t\t\t// Store in an index for the config's namespace\n  1709→\t\t\t// a proxy from this namespace will first look here for the destination rule for a given service\n  1710→\t\t\t// This pool consists of both public/private destination rules.\n  1711→\t\t\tif _, exist := namespaceLocalDestRules[configs[i].Namespace]; !exist {\n  1712→\t\t\t\tnamespaceLocalDestRules[configs[i].Namespace] = newProcessedDestRules()\n  1713→\t\t\t}\n  1714→\t\t\t// Merge this destination rule with any public/private dest rules for same host in the same namespace\n  1715→\t\t\t// If there are no duplicates, the dest rule will be added to the list\n  1716→\t\t\tps.mergeDestinationRule(namespaceLocalDestRules[configs[i].Namespace], configs[i], exportToMap)\n  1717→\t\t}\n  1718→\n  1719→\t\tisPrivateOnly := false\n  1720→\t\t// No exportTo in destinationRule. Use the global default\n  1721→\t\t// We only honor . and *\n  1722→\t\tif len(rule.ExportTo) == 0 && ps.exportToDefaults.destinationRule[visibility.Private] {\n  1723→\t\t\tisPrivateOnly = true\n  1724→\t\t} else if len(rule.ExportTo) == 1 && (exportToMap[visibility.Private]) {\n  1725→\t\t\tisPrivateOnly = true\n  1726→\t\t}\n  1727→\n  1728→\t\t// If destination rule has a workloadSelector set, visibility should be private.\n  1729→\t\tif rule.GetWorkloadSelector() != nil {\n  1730→\t\t\tisPrivateOnly = true\n  1731→\t\t}\n  1732→\n  1733→\t\tif !isPrivateOnly {\n  1734→\t\t\tif _, exist := exportedDestRulesByNamespace[configs[i].Namespace]; !exist {\n  1735→\t\t\t\texportedDestRulesByNamespace[configs[i].Namespace] = newProcessedDestRules()\n  1736→\t\t\t}\n  1737→\t\t\t// Merge this destination rule with any other exported dest rule for the same host in the same namespace\n  1738→\t\t\t// If there are no duplicates, the dest rule will be added to the list\n  1739→\t\t\tps.mergeDestinationRule(exportedDestRulesByNamespace[configs[i].Namespace], configs[i], exportToMap)\n  1740→\t\t} else if configs[i].Namespace == ps.Mesh.RootNamespace {\n  1741→\t\t\t// Keep track of private root namespace destination rules\n  1742→\t\t\tps.mergeDestinationRule(rootNamespaceLocalDestRules, configs[i], exportToMap)\n  1743→\t\t}\n  1744→\t}\n  1745→\n  1746→\t// precompute DestinationRules with inherited fields\n  1747→\tif features.EnableDestinationRuleInheritance {\n  1748→\t\tglobalRule := inheritedConfigs[ps.Mesh.RootNamespace]\n  1749→\t\tfor ns := range namespaceLocalDestRules {\n  1750→\t\t\tnsRule := inheritedConfigs[ns]\n  1751→\t\t\tinheritedRule := ps.inheritDestinationRule(globalRule, nsRule)\n  1752→\t\t\tfor hostname, cfgList := range namespaceLocalDestRules[ns].destRules {\n  1753→\t\t\t\tfor i, cfg := range cfgList {\n  1754→\t\t\t\t\tnamespaceLocalDestRules[ns].destRules[hostname][i] = ps.inheritDestinationRule(inheritedRule, cfg)\n  1755→\t\t\t\t}\n  1756→\t\t\t}\n  1757→\t\t\t// update namespace rule after it has been merged with mesh rule\n  1758→\t\t\tinheritedConfigs[ns] = inheritedRule\n  1759→\t\t}\n  1760→\t\t// can't precalculate exportedDestRulesByNamespace since we don't know all the client namespaces in advance\n  1761→\t\t// inheritance is performed in getExportedDestinationRuleFromNamespace\n  1762→\t}\n  1763→\n  1764→\tps.destinationRuleIndex.namespaceLocal = namespaceLocalDestRules\n  1765→\tps.destinationRuleIndex.exportedByNamespace = exportedDestRulesByNamespace\n  1766→\tps.destinationRuleIndex.rootNamespaceLocal = rootNamespaceLocalDestRules\n  1767→\tps.destinationRuleIndex.inheritedByNamespace = inheritedConfigs\n  1768→}\n  1769→\n  1770→func (ps *PushContext) initAuthorizationPolicies(env *Environment) error {\n  1771→\tvar err error\n  1772→\tif ps.AuthzPolicies, err = GetAuthorizationPolicies(env); err != nil {\n  1773→\t\tauthzLog.Errorf(\"failed to initialize authorization policies: %v\", err)\n  1774→\t\treturn err\n  1775→\t}\n  1776→\treturn nil\n  1777→}\n  1778→\n  1779→func (ps *PushContext) 1782→\t\treturn\n  1783→\t}\n  1784→\treturn\n  1785→}\n  1786→\n  1787→func (ps *PushContext) initProxyConfigs(env *Environment) error {\n  1788→\tvar err error\n  1789→\tif ps.ProxyConfigs, err = 1794→}\n  1795→\n  1796→// pre computes WasmPlugins per namespace\n  1797→func (ps *PushContext) initWasmPlugins(env *Environment) error {\n  1798→\twasmplugins, err := env.List(gvk.WasmPlugin, NamespaceAll)\n  1799→\tif err != nil {\n  1800→\t\treturn err\n  1801→\t}\n  1802→\n  1803→\tsortConfigByCreationTime(wasmplugins)\n  1804→\tps.wasmPluginsByNamespace = map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper{}\n  1805→\tfor _, plugin := range wasmplugins {\n  1806→\t\tif pluginWrapper := convertToWasmPluginWrapper(&plugin); pluginWrapper != nil {\n  1807→\t\t\tps.wasmPluginsByNamespace[plugin.Namespace] = append(ps.wasmPluginsByNamespace[plugin.Namespace], pluginWrapper)\n  1808→\t\t}\n  1809→\t}\n  1810→\n  1811→\treturn nil\n  1812→}\n  1813→\n  1814→// WasmPlugins return the WasmPluginWrappers of a proxy\n  1815→func (ps *PushContext) WasmPlugins(proxy *Proxy) map[extensions.PluginPhase][]*WasmPluginWrapper {\n  1816→\tif proxy == nil {\n  1817→\t\treturn nil\n  1818→\t}\n  1819→\tvar workloadLabels labels.Collection\n  1820→\tif proxy.Metadata != nil && len(proxy.Metadata.Labels) > 0 {\n  1821→\t\tworkloadLabels = labels.Collection{proxy.Metadata.Labels}\n  1822→\t}\n  1823→\tmatchedPlugins := make(map[extensions.PluginPhase][]*WasmPluginWrapper)\n  1824→\t// First get all the extension configs from the config root namespace\n  1825→\t// and then add the ones from proxy's own namespace\n  1826→\tif ps.Mesh.RootNamespace != \"\" {\n  1827→\t\t// if there is no workload selector, the config applies to all workloads\n  1828→\t\t// if there is a workload selector, check for matching workload labels\n  1829→\t\tfor _, plugin := range ps.wasmPluginsByNamespace[ps.Mesh.RootNamespace] {\n  1830→\t\t\tif plugin.Selector == nil || workloadLabels.IsSupersetOf(plugin.Selector.MatchLabels) {\n  1831→\t\t\t\tmatchedPlugins[plugin.Phase] = append(matchedPlugins[plugin.Phase], plugin)\n  1832→\t\t\t}\n  1833→\t\t}\n  1834→\t}\n  1835→\n  1836→\t// To prevent duplicate extensions in case root namespace equals proxy's namespace\n  1837→\tif proxy.ConfigNamespace != ps.Mesh.RootNamespace {\n  1838→\t\tfor _, plugin := range ps.wasmPluginsByNamespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace] {\n  1839→\t\t\tif plugin.Selector == nil || workloadLabels.IsSupersetOf(plugin.Selector.MatchLabels) {\n  1840→\t\t\t\tmatchedPlugins[plugin.Phase] = append(matchedPlugins[plugin.Phase], plugin)\n  1841→\t\t\t}\n  1842→\t\t}\n  1843→\t}\n  1844→\n  1845→\t// sort slices by priority\n  1846→\tfor i, slice := range matchedPlugins {\n  1847→\t\tsort.SliceStable(slice, func(i, j int) bool {\n  1848→\t\t\tiPriority := int64(math.MinInt64)\n  1849→\t\t\tif prio := slice[i].Priority; prio != nil {\n  1850→\t\t\t\tiPriority = prio.Value\n  1851→\t\t\t}\n  1852→\t\t\tjPriority := int64(math.MinInt64)\n  1853→\t\t\tif prio := slice[j].Priority; prio != nil {\n  1854→\t\t\t\tjPriority = prio.Value\n  1855→\t\t\t}\n  1856→\t\t\treturn iPriority > jPriority\n  1857→\t\t})\n  1858→\t\tmatchedPlugins[i] = slice\n  1859→\t}\n  1860→\n  1861→\treturn matchedPlugins\n  1862→}\n  1863→\n  1864→// pre computes envoy filters per namespace\n  1865→func (ps *PushContext) initEnvoyFilters(env *Environment) error {\n  1866→\tenvoyFilterConfigs, err := env.List(gvk.EnvoyFilter, NamespaceAll)\n  1867→\tif err != nil {\n  1868→\t\treturn err\n  1869→\t}\n  1870→\n  1871→\tsort.Slice(envoyFilterConfigs, func(i, j int) bool {\n  1872→\t\tifilter := envoyFilterConfigs[i].Spec.(*networking.EnvoyFilter)\n  1873→\t\tjfilter := envoyFilterConfigs[j].Spec.(*networking.EnvoyFilter)\n  1874→\t\tif ifilter.Priority != jfilter.Priority {\n  1875→\t\t\treturn ifilter.Priority < jfilter.Priority\n  1876→\t\t}\n  1877→\t\t// If priority is same fallback to name and creation timestamp, else use priority.\n  1878→\t\t// If creation time is the same, then behavior is nondeterministic. In this case, we can\n  1879→\t\t// pick an arbitrary but consistent ordering based on name and namespace, which is unique.\n  1880→\t\t// CreationTimestamp is stored in seconds, so this is not uncommon.\n  1881→\t\tif envoyFilterConfigs[i].CreationTimestamp != envoyFilterConfigs[j].CreationTimestamp {\n  1882→\t\t\treturn envoyFilterConfigs[i].CreationTimestamp.Before(envoyFilterConfigs[j].CreationTimestamp)\n  1883→\t\t}\n  1884→\t\tin := envoyFilterConfigs[i].Name + \".\" + envoyFilterConfigs[i].Namespace\n  1885→\t\tjn := envoyFilterConfigs[j].Name + \".\" + envoyFilterConfigs[j].Namespace\n  1886→\t\treturn in < jn\n  1887→\t})\n  1888→\n  1889→\tps.envoyFiltersByNamespace = make(map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper)\n  1890→\tfor _, envoyFilterConfig := range envoyFilterConfigs {\n  1891→\t\tefw := convertToEnvoyFilterWrapper(&envoyFilterConfig)\n  1892→\t\tif _, exists := ps.envoyFiltersByNamespace[envoyFilterConfig.Namespace]; !exists {\n  1893→\t\t\tps.envoyFiltersByNamespace[envoyFilterConfig.Namespace] = make([]*EnvoyFilterWrapper, 0)\n  1894→\t\t}\n  1895→\t\tps.envoyFiltersByNamespace[envoyFilterConfig.Namespace] = append(ps.envoyFiltersByNamespace[envoyFilterConfig.Namespace], efw)\n  1896→\t}\n  1897→\treturn nil\n  1898→}\n  1899→\n  1900→// EnvoyFilters return the merged EnvoyFilterWrapper of a proxy\n  1901→func (ps *PushContext) EnvoyFilters(proxy *Proxy) *EnvoyFilterWrapper {\n  1902→\t// this should never happen\n  1903→\tif proxy == nil {\n  1904→\t\treturn nil\n  1905→\t}\n  1906→\tvar matchedEnvoyFilters []*EnvoyFilterWrapper\n  1907→\t// EnvoyFilters supports inheritance (global ones plus namespace local ones).\n  1908→\t// First get all the filter configs from the config root namespace\n  1909→\t// and then add the ones from proxy's own namespace\n  1910→\tif ps.Mesh.RootNamespace != \"\" {\n  1911→\t\tmatchedEnvoyFilters = ps.getMatchedEnvoyFilters(proxy, ps.Mesh.RootNamespace)\n  1912→\t}\n  1913→\n  1914→\t// To prevent duplicate envoyfilters in case root namespace equals proxy's namespace\n  1915→\tif proxy.ConfigNamespace != ps.Mesh.RootNamespace {\n  1916→\t\tmatched := ps.getMatchedEnvoyFilters(proxy, proxy.ConfigNamespace)\n  1917→\t\tmatchedEnvoyFilters = append(matchedEnvoyFilters, matched...)\n  1918→\t}\n  1919→\n  1920→\tvar out *EnvoyFilterWrapper\n  1921→\tif len(matchedEnvoyFilters) > 0 {\n  1922→\t\tout = &EnvoyFilterWrapper{\n  1923→\t\t\t// no need populate workloadSelector, as it is not used later.\n  1924→\t\t\tPatches: make(map[networking.EnvoyFilter_ApplyTo][]*EnvoyFilterConfigPatchWrapper),\n  1925→\t\t}\n  1926→\t\t// merge EnvoyFilterWrapper\n  1927→\t\tfor _, efw := range matchedEnvoyFilters {\n  1928→\t\t\tfor applyTo, cps := range efw.Patches {\n  1929→\t\t\t\tfor _, cp := range cps {\n  1930→\t\t\t\t\tif proxyMatch(proxy, cp) {\n  1931→\t\t\t\t\t\tout.Patches[applyTo] = append(out.Patches[applyTo], cp)\n  1932→\t\t\t\t\t}\n  1933→\t\t\t\t}\n  1934→\t\t\t}\n  1935→\t\t}\n  1936→\t}\n  1937→\n  1938→\treturn out\n  1939→}\n  1940→\n  1941→// if there is no workload selector, the config applies to all workloads\n  1942→// if there is a workload selector, check for matching workload labels\n  1943→func (ps *PushContext) getMatchedEnvoyFilters(proxy *Proxy, namespaces string) []*EnvoyFilterWrapper {\n  1944→\tmatchedEnvoyFilters := make([]*EnvoyFilterWrapper, 0)\n  1945→\tfor _, efw := range ps.envoyFiltersByNamespace[namespaces] {\n  1946→\t\tvar workloadLabels labels.Collection\n  1947→\t\tif proxy.Metadata != nil && len(proxy.Metadata.Labels) > 0 {\n  1948→\t\t\tworkloadLabels = labels.Collection{proxy.Metadata.Labels}\n  1949→\t\t}\n  1950→\t\tif efw.workloadSelector == nil || workloadLabels.IsSupersetOf(efw.workloadSelector) {\n  1951→\t\t\tmatchedEnvoyFilters = append(matchedEnvoyFilters, efw)\n  1952→\t\t}\n  1953→\t}\n  1954→\treturn matchedEnvoyFilters\n  1955→}\n  1956→\n  1957→// HasEnvoyFilters checks if an EnvoyFilter exists with the given name at the given namespace.\n  1958→func (ps *PushContext) HasEnvoyFilters(name, namespace string) bool {\n  1959→\tfor _, efw := range ps.envoyFiltersByNamespace[namespace] {\n  1960→\t\tif efw.Name == name {\n  1961→\t\t\treturn true\n  1962→\t\t}\n  1963→\t}\n  1964→\treturn false\n  1965→}\n  1966→\n  1967→// pre computes gateways per namespace\n  1968→func (ps *PushContext) initGateways(env *Environment) error {\n  1969→\tgatewayConfigs, err := env.List(gvk.Gateway, NamespaceAll)\n  1970→\tif err != nil {\n  1971→\t\treturn err\n  1972→\t}\n  1973→\n  1974→\tsortConfigByCreationTime(gatewayConfigs)\n  1975→\n  1976→\tif features.ScopeGatewayToNamespace {\n  1977→\t\tps.gatewayIndex.namespace = make(map[string][]config.Config)\n  1978→\t\tfor _, gatewayConfig := range gatewayConfigs {\n  1979→\t\t\tif _, exists := ps.gatewayIndex.namespace[gatewayConfig.Namespace]; !exists {\n  1980→\t\t\t\tps.gatewayIndex.namespace[gatewayConfig.Namespace] = make([]config.Config, 0)\n  1981→\t\t\t}\n  1982→\t\t\tps.gatewayIndex.namespace[gatewayConfig.Namespace] = append(ps.gatewayIndex.namespace[gatewayConfig.Namespace], gatewayConfig)\n  1983→\t\t}\n  1984→\t} else {\n  1985→\t\tps.gatewayIndex.all = gatewayConfigs\n  1986→\t}\n  1987→\treturn nil\n  1988→}\n  1989→\n  1990→// InternalGatewayServiceAnnotation represents the hostname of the service a gateway will use. This is\n  1991→// only used internally to transfer information from the Kubernetes Gateway API to the Istio Gateway API\n  1992→// which does not have a field to represent this.\n  1993→// The format is a comma separated list of hostnames. For example, \"ingress.istio-system.svc.cluster.local,ingress.example.com\"\n  1994→// The Gateway will apply to all ServiceInstances of these services, *in the same namespace as the Gateway*.\n  1995→const InternalGatewayServiceAnnotation = \"internal.istio.io/gateway-service\"\n  1996→\n  1997→type gatewayWithInstances struct {\n  1998→\tgateway config.Config\n  1999→\t// If true, ports that are not present in any instance will be used directly (without targetPort translation)\n  2000→\t// This supports the legacy behavior of selecting gateways by pod label selector\n  2001→\tlegacyGatewaySelector bool\n  2002→\tinstances             []*ServiceInstance\n  2003→}\n  2004→\n  2005→func (ps *PushContext) mergeGateways(proxy *Proxy) *MergedGateway {\n  2006→\t// this should never happen\n  2007→\tif proxy == nil {\n  2008→\t\treturn nil\n  2009→\t}\n  2010→\tgatewayInstances := make([]gatewayWithInstances, 0)\n  2011→\n  2012→\tvar configs []config.Config\n  2013→\tif features.ScopeGatewayToNamespace {\n  2014→\t\tconfigs = ps.gatewayIndex.namespace[proxy.ConfigNamespace]\n  2015→\t} else {\n  2016→\t\tconfigs = ps.gatewayIndex.all\n  2017→\t}\n  2018→\n  2019→\tfor _, cfg := range configs {\n  2020→\t\tgw := cfg.Spec.(*networking.Gateway)\n  2021→\t\tif gwsvcstr, f := cfg.Annotations[InternalGatewayServiceAnnotation];
